{\n\tt.Helper()\n\n\trcache.SetupForTest(t)\n\tredispool.SetupForTest(t, tenanttest.TestContext())\n\n\tcf, save := httptestutil.NewRecorderFactory(t, update(name), name)\n\tdoer, err := cf.Doer()\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatal(err)\n\t}\n\n\tbaseURL, err := url.Parse(\"https://gitlab.com/\")\n\tif err != nil {\n\t\tt.Fatal(err)\n\t}\n\n\tprovider := NewClientProvider(\"TestVCR\", baseURL, doer)\n\n\t// Try to use a token if available for VCR recording, otherwise use unauthenticated\n\ttoken := \"\"\n\tif vcrToken != nil && vcrToken.Token != \"\" {\n\t\ttoken = vcrToken.Token\n\t}\n\n\tcli := provider.GetOAuthClient(token)\n\tcli.internalRateLimiter = ratelimit.NewInstrumentedLimiter(\"gitlab\", rate.NewLimiter(100, 10))\n\n\treturn cli, save\n}\n\nfunc
